<username>Mei Fu Lee</username><Date>1562041137942</Date>< rating>
3</rating>
< text>
My friends love mongolian noodles so they begged to come here. I didnt really know what they meant but realized when I saw the layout. Mongolian bbq! Between 3 of us, we shared two entree (the cheapest option), which also came with a free extra noodles. The register gave us two bowls to fill up with meat, veggies, and sauces.

We got almost everything. I really appreciated the variety of toppings. The bar was also really clean. We got to the end and were ready to give it, but the man made us go all the way around the island to give it to him. He cooked it and added the extra noodles to one dish.

There was a lot of seating in the mall. The food was good, the beef tasted like jerky. We added pineapple and lemon to one dish to make it a little sweeter and it was really good! This is a simple place and the food is not bad.< /text>

<userid>112479929658549938845</userid><user_name>Tom Lee</user_name>< Review>
I've been going here a long time and it's one of my favorite little hidden gems.  I've loathed telling other than close friends about this place cause it's small and can get too crowded sometimes and I get turned away at times showing up without a reservation... but it's time to grow up and stop being so selfish.  Sushi is authentic and reasonably priced, cash only, no non-sense kind of place.  There's better top of the line sushi at other high end places but Okina's combination of price, freshness, preparation and cozy experience makes it a 5 star place in my book.  Hard to find due to little signage and hard to park, but worth the trouble.  Japanese owner chef is talented and sometimes talkative, sometimes not and it helps to stay on his good side : )</Review>

<review>I was strolling along with the wife and we decided to check out renting some bikes.  My wife wanted more a regular bike and I wanted to be able to use some power.  The bikes let you do both (and they DO carry non-electric bikes too for rent).  After trying both, we went electric since Eddie advised we don't do 1 electric and 1 non-electric.  The ones we got don't have pedal assist - it was only pedal OR throttle.

Eddie was VERY friendly and helpful.  He provided a paper map and gave us some tips on where to relax, etc.  The rates are very reasonable - they don't offer a half day rate but if you rent it for 3-4 hours, it ends up being the same or less.  PLUS I think the other places charge you up front whereas these guys charge you when you return (and seem to be flexible on how they track time).  They also may have a discount depending on which hotel you're staying at.

They lend you bike locks and clean helmets.

Thanks, Eddie!!!

I would highly recommend!!<//review>< pics>
None<//pics>

< Text>
So my family and I were looking for something NEW to do in San Diego and we thought we would rent bikes and go for a ride. On our way to the bike rental place I saw a sign that said "electric biked" and said... BETTER! :) Just incase we got tired or peddling if we went too far.

So we meet this really awesome guy names Sean who not only took a good amount of time explaining how things worked but also gave us a more than fair rate and got us ready for our ride. Also providing helmets for the children and a special seat for my 2 year old.

Never rode an electric bike before but all I can say is that it was easy! It was set so I can peddle and throttle the power if needed. Just a wonderful bike to ride.

The subsequent contacts with the following older women were absolutely prejudicial and inappropriate at times. As in, the worker sat on my couch and refused to leave my home until it was signed, despite the fact that the contract was supposedly "voluntary". Further an another contact by another older worker was met with near hostility and threats of their ability to remove my children.. (please note an initial contact was with a supervisor who clearly stated that despite the public opinion of cps they were not about removing children but rather keeping children safe in their home), upon receipt of the records of the last contact, (you have to petition the court at the juvenile hall fyi) the worker unethically misconstrued several statements and failed to report several contacts made via phone, and stated to the father of my child, that if cps were to remove my children by means of him making a complaint, its would be obvious that they would be placed with their father. She equally closed my case given the lack of evidence, "substantiated" the claim without sufficient evidence, and will hopefully hear from her supervisor after I make a formal complaint. Its never a positive thing dealing with child protective services, but the unethical, and abuse of power that was given makes them incapable in my opinion to remember what their job was in the first place. As one supervisor told me, workers are still people, some are good and some are bad. But maybe if I ever do come across any again, I'll be sure to remind them that unlike some of their other cases, I'm not only surrounded by mandated reporters myself, but am in the wait list for a county job that requires me to mandate report.<//Text>

Oddly, they were able to walk a drink out to us but the girl said she thought we already got our food and did not walk food back out but instead directed us to go through the drive-thru.
Wow...  Totally love cold fries... doesn't everyone?

3/5/18 - 4 stars

This McDs remodeled itself maybe a couple of years ago now. Opened up with a beautiful new building. However, at the time of the remodel, they removed the chocolate flavor from their swirl cone. So now, it‚Äôs vanilla only, rather than vanilla-chocolate mix. But aside from that disappointing change, everything else has been an improvement.

The dual drive thru lines are great, even though some other customers have no idea how to merge politely. But not a big deal since you never seem to be in the line long anyhow, as food comes out hot and fast.

8/5/20 - 2 stars

So when you order on the mobile app you can no longer go inside to pick up, and you can't change this option once selected. So if you don't pick curbside delivery and enter your strap number, they make you wait in the drive-thru line which today took a total of 18 minutes after our order was placed. So we are left with cold fries in our car right now...
Oddly, they were able to walk a drink out to us but the girl said she thought we already got our food and did not walk food back out but instead directed us to go through the drive-thru.
Wow...  Totally love cold fries... doesn't everyone?

3/5/18 - 4 stars

This McDs remodeled itself maybe a couple of years ago now. Opened up with a beautiful new building. However, at the time of the remodel, they removed the chocolate flavor from their swirl cone. So now, it‚Äôs vanilla only, rather than vanilla-chocolate mix. But aside from that disappointing change, everything else has been an improvement.

The dual drive thru lines are great, even though some other customers have no idea how to merge politely. But not a big deal since you never seem to be in the line long anyhow, as food comes out hot and fast.

We weren‚Äôt the only ones thinking about ice cream sundaes and shakes last night; the car in front of us had the same order. Vanilla swirl cones ($1.62 each). So good!< /text>
